	\e[34m
	______________________________________________________
	\e[39m
	Welcome to the IT340 midterm
	\e[34m
	Instructions
	\e[39m
	You'll need to complete a number of tasks in the given time (approx 90 minutes)
	\e[32m
	Prereq:\e[39m
		Once you log in, make sure you run 'script mywork.txt -f' so it can record your progress.
	When you're done with the midterm do ctrl+d to stop script, or stop the process, if done correctly you should see output mentioning it stopped. 
	(Don't do ctrl+d too often as you'll log yourself out)
	Properly recording via mywork.txt \e[31m (1 point)\e[39m
		If you forget to do script, make sure you do history > mywork.txt
	Load the resulting output to github at the end of the midterm.
	
	\e[32m
	First \e[39m 
	Inspect the system as there are a number of performance issues (4 issues)
	Use the commands we learned about in class to find and fix/stop the issues.
	You must record the following details:
		What the detected issue was. \e[31m (1 point for each)\e[39m
		Details of where/how you found it. \e[31m (1 point for each)\e[39m
		How you resolved it. \e[31m (1 point for each)\e[39m
	\e[32m
	
	Second \e[39m 
	Install and configure Apache. 
	Properly configure Virtualbox and Apache so you can access it from your host machine similar to the Nagios lab.
	Edit the default index file in the default location:
		Change the file extension to .php \e[31m (1 point)\e[39m
		Erase all the content and replace it with the following \e[31m (1 point)\e[39m:
		\e[32m <?php echo 'Hello world, Midterm<br>' . date; ?> \e[39m
		Capture a screenshot of this page rendered on your host machine's browser, make sure you show the url. \e[31m (1 point)\e[39m
			This will be the proof of the previous steps.
		Make note of the process/steps you needed to do to accomplish this.
		If you ran into any issues explain what they were and how you resolved them.
			Details about the issue(s) and the steps/resolution: \e[31m (10 points)\e[39m
			
	\e[32m
	Third \e[39m 
	Properly setup a cron job that'll update and upgrade the system every 15 minutes.
		Take a screenshot of the cron file with your cron definition. \e[31m (1 point)\e[39m
		Keep a copy of the script showing the commands that the job will run (save to github) \e[31m (1 point)\e[39m
		
	\e[32m
	Fourth \e[39m 
	Install and configure rsyslog to send Apache logs to ~/log directory. 
		Screenshot the result of 'ls ~/log' once setup and working. \e[31m (1 point)\e[39m
		Configure it as shown in class by making new config files instead of directly editing the rsys.conf. \e[31m (1 point)\e[39m
			These scripts will go on github.
			
	\e[31m
	For recording your data:
		You can either clone your git directory and copy all relevant data to your repository
		or you can move all relevant files to the /vagrant folder then you can access them on your host machine and manually upload the data.
	Make sure you gather all the requirements before you logout and do vagrant destroy.
	
	Good luck!
	For your reference you can find the instructions again at \e[32m /home/vagrant/instructions.txt
	\e[39m
